<review>I'm 35 years old and finally decided to make the call to Lasik Vision Institute after hearing how good lasik has been to people I work with. So, I had my lasik surgery on July 19. It was way better than what I thought it was going to be. Dr. Bavand made me feel comfortable and I did not feel a thing ( they provided plenty of numbing medication and sedative). Dr. Bavand let me know what he was doing every step of the way. I felt like I was under his surgical care in less than 10 minutes. I have had two follow up appointments and Rose checks me in and gets me ready to see Dr. Nguyen. Rose and Dr. Nguyen make it a pleasant visit answering all my questions and addressing what post follow up care I need to pay closer attention to. This office is very professional and clean. I remember reading how dry the eyes feel after having this surgery. I experienced super dry eyes the first couple of weeks along with light sensitivity during the day, and glare at night. I would use the drops as instructed, all day, and also would wear the dark eye shades( sunglasses) they provided me throughout the day, even at work on the computer. Now that I am 2 months post surgery, I use the drops 4-6 times a day, and wear my sunglasses when driving. I have no issues with glare at night. The eye drops they recommended are those daily use vials that I bought at Costco. They feel soo good. keep your eyes moist! Lots of Omega-3 people! If you are thinking about Lasik, I say go for it! <name>Aries franhens</name><review>Disclaimer: I had my surgery Oct. 2017.

I remember everything as it happened yesterday! I wanted to get the Lasik done for such a long time, but looking for the right Dr. To perform the procedure took me a long time to find. I seriously had  so many consultations with Doctors all over southern California but none ever felt right. It wasn't until I had my first consultation with Dr. Melikian and his amazing team! ( Dr. Nguyen , Beverly, Jonas and Rose) that I fell in love with the place and I knew I wanted to have my surgery with them. When I met with the doctor for the first time, I had a list of questions I asked every doctor I would meet, and Dr. Melik was super patient with me and my mom; answer; he every single question and  concern we had, was throughout and above all, he had the best attitude, bedside manners and he was just super super nice. The whole team was and has always been extremely nice and welcoming, which is something that almost never happens at  doctors offices.

The procedure
If you have been doing your research, you will know the procedure itself is very quick ( I recommend watching YouTube videos). On the day of the surgery they ask you to come dress comfortably, which I did, because after the procedure they are going to prescribe you a sedative(if I'm not mistaken) that will help with any pain and will help you sleep it off until the next day).  So you come in in the morning, they are going to make you watch a video of what's going to happen and what to expect after. The team will give you a care packet with eye wear you must wear for some good two weeks post lasik (to not accidentally rub your eyes when you sleep). A fter all the videos and explanations, I was super excited to start and to be honest I was not scared or nervous at all! but they will offer you and recommend you to take a relaxer pill. Which I did but I kinda regret taking because it obviously makes you Druggy and relaxed, but I just hate feeling of dizziness so this is a personal choice.
The procedure seriously lasts like 5 seconds each eye approximately. It's ridiculously short! It made me regret all the years it took me to made up my mind to get the surgery done. I walked in with blurry vision, and 5 minutes later I walked out ...well still with watery blurry vision but it was much better than before xD. I then walked out all happy and excited, took the medication to knock me out for the day and I slept the day away until the next morning.
I did not feel any pain at all, I don't know if that's usual but I had no pain , no headache and my eyes looked great! There was no sign that I had just had lasik done. I could see crystal clear! For the first time since I was 11 years old, I did not have to reach out to grab my glasses first thing when I woke up in the morning. It was so amazing, having HD vision, see signs that were fAr away ! It is seriously a life changing decision. I have no regrets up to this day! My eyes did end up being dry and I do have to use eye drops multiple times a day. If I stay too long without eye drops, I do get pretty bad headache. They say that normally it does away with time, but I just happen to have the bad luck that it has not. The doctor gives you alternatives, like eye plugs, which definitely help SOOOOO much! Look them up, they are very handy. It is really hard to live with dry eyes, but at the same time having great vision is so amazing and for me kinda worth the dryness.
Up to this date, I still visit Dr. Nguyen and Dr.Melik for follow ups to make sure my eyes health is still goodand Make sure my sight is clear and amazing. I am still really happy with the results, even though my eyes are really dry.< /review><gmap_id>0x80dd27f3686dfda9:0xbb8fd03b88448106<//gmap_id><user_id>113259038639884674775< /user_id><Rating>5</Rating></record>

I got PRK last year (exactly a year ago), and I am so glad I did! I've been able to enjoy the super bloom this spring, and also not have to keep on buying glasses every time my boyfriend sits on them!

The process was easy. My mom previously got her lasik here several years ago, and my dad also came to this office for lasik many many years ago. So I knew i wanted to come to this office for my eyes! My mom decided to gift me the gift of vision as my graduation present. So i made an appointment for a consultation, and a few weeks later, I came in and got the PRK done! During the surgery, the doctors are really good with keeping you relaxed and calm, and talk you through the WHOLE process every step of the way.  Healing time took awhile. Within two weeks, i was able to see clearer but it took about two months for my eyes to adjust completely. So if you're thinking about getting PRK, make sure you're able to get someone to take care of you for awhile (like driving) so you wont have to deal with being blind.  They also offer regular checkups to make sure your eyes are healing fine after the surgery.

The staff here are amazing! Evelyn and Jonas in the front are very helpful and always accommodating. Dr. Nguyen and Dr. Melikian are so nice and knowledgeable. Awesome office!</Review>

< Review>
This farmers market is a nice size where you can get in and get out in about an hour give or take.  The variety of offerings is not the most robust I've seen, but the prices and choices that are available could probably fulfill ~85% of your general grocery needs.  The products too are generally quality and fresh, and the farmers are super accommodating with allowing use of your own reusable packing.  There is also a small selection of pre-prepared foods, baked goods, and even a fish monger type stall.

There's also a decent amount of parking available in lots and on streets that do not require pay, so bonus!</Review>

< Review>
Got the 12+ year old fence repaired, powered washed, sanded and stained. The service was outstanding and result is marvelous. The old stain on the 300 ft long fence was solid maroon and became very inconsistent due to weathering. Stripping the solid stain and heavy mildew was no easy task. Originally, I thought that it had to be covered with an even darker semi-solid stain. After the treatment and power washing, it looked hopeful that the fence can take on a semi-transparent to show the beautiful wood grains. Luis took up the challenge: not only a semi-transparent stain, but also a very bright "cedar stain" from Armstrong. It took a lot of sanding to remove the remaining stubborn red stain in preparation and apply a second coat in certain areas to make up the differences in fence wood quality due to weathering. Now the fence looks new and boasts nice wood grains with consistent color across the yard.

Luis is the most thoughtful and responsive contractor manager that I have ever encountered. The initial inspection was meticulous and the estimate was detailed. He responded to questions and concerns very quickly. He is also very flexible with the schedule allowing time for rain to dry and us to decide on the color. His crew are very nice and care deeply about the quality of their work.< /Review>
